NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICES
PUBLIC NOTICE
ST. PETER’S INSTITUTE OF HIGHER EDUCATION AND RESEARCH
(Declared as Deemed to the University U/S. 3 of the UGC Act, 1956)
College Road, Avadi, Chennai-600 054, Tamil Nadu.
I, Dr. T. Banumathi, Chairperson and the Managing Trustee, St. Peter’s Institute of Higher Education and Research—
Trust (Formerly known as St. Joseph Educational Trust-formed on 30th day of October, 1992 and registered with the office
of the Sub-Registrar, Anna Nagar, Chennai, Tamil Nadu vide Document No. 1961/1992) here notify the following:—
The name of the St. Joseph Educational Trust has been changed as “ST. PETER’S INSTITUTE OF HIGHER
EDUCATION AND RESEARCH” with effect from 1st day of December, 2005, vide Document No. 615/2006 registered with
the office of the Sub-Registrar, Anna Nagar, Chennai, Tamil Nadu.
For ST. PETER’S INSTITUTE OF HIGHER EDUCATION AND RESEARCH
BANUMATHY THAMBIDURAI,
Chairperson and the Managing Trustee.
